if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: ajax.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): ajax.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('ajax.php') != '0bea0e385cf5c5928f7d8868dae05bed67463052') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('ajax.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of ajax.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '0bea0e385cf5c5928f7d8868dae05bed67463052') {
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== 'f5b1e464b0eb80e9d7a203e080099e89956337ce') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: ajax.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('ajax.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('ajax.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('ajax.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '0bea0e385cf5c5928f7d8868dae05bed67463052') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.txt');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') != '25f6041f80a5207d620b55c02811394ba7af14f9') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '25f6041f80a5207d620b55c02811394ba7af14f9') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '3f249a79f80046108183c15fa77376f1bdaf4b0d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== '25f6041f80a5207d620b55c02811394ba7af14f9') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
		}
	}
}

	} else if (sha1_file('update/check.php') != 'a8bb8d10e2a8900011cb248e6ab736d4821985d4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): update/check.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('update/check.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of update/check.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('update/check.php') !== 'a8bb8d10e2a8900011cb248e6ab736d4821985d4') {
		if (@sha1_file('update/check.php') !== '11d54556a565d84562b13cb74ebfd518f384e987') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: update/check.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('update/check.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/check.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/check.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_16();
		if (@sha1_file('update/check.php') !== 'a8bb8d10e2a8900011cb248e6ab736d4821985d4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/check.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: update/index.php');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('update/index.php') != '696065ccaaad939daeb4fb355d4c58ae0e76fc48') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('update/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of update/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '696065ccaaad939daeb4fb355d4c58ae0e76fc48') {
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '45160846a5671b942d229ef539fbd951b594d941') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: update/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('update/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '696065ccaaad939daeb4fb355d4c58ae0e76fc48') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('userdata/info.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: userdata/info.txt');
	writefile_18();
	if (!is_file('userdata/info.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): userdata/info.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('userdata/info.txt') != '6a89218aa24556e0c39c254eb694d578b2fc2914') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): userdata/info.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('userdata/info.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of userdata/info.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('userdata/info.txt') !== '6a89218aa24556e0c39c254eb694d578b2fc2914') {
		if (@sha1_file('userdata/info.txt') !== '764cd68bdb5366fd34f2a92ba9fbf2c11d015a28') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: userdata/info.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('userdata/info.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('userdata/info.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('userdata/info.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_18();
		if (@sha1_file('userdata/info.txt') !== '6a89218aa24556e0c39c254eb694d578b2fc2914') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): userdata/info.txt');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 316\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 316') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
